M ea su r e an d m ap h o w mu c h c arb o n t h ese ecos ys t em s c u rre n t ly st o r e, u sin g glob ally re c o gn iz ed s t an d ard s su c h as Pla n V ivo a n d IPCC g u id eli n es. 3. D evelo p a c lea r, c o mmu n it y - i n volved sy st em f o r mo n it o rin g, re p o r t in g, a n d verif yi n g ( M RV) t h e st a t e o f t h ese ecosys t em s an d t h ei r c ar b o n st o rag e. 4. Pr o vid e a p la t f o rm t h at en ab l es re al - t ime mo n i t o rin g o f t h e vari o u s eco sy st em s f o r p ro mp t d ecision - mak in g an d ac t ion s 5. I d en t if y an d p rio ri t iz e are as n ee d in g re st o rat i o n an d re c o mme n d a p p ro p ria t e re st o ra t io n me t h o d s. 6. D evelo p c lea r t er ms o f r ef ere n c e t o r ecru i t an ex p ert c o n su l t an t t o c re a t e a d et ail ed re st o ra t io n st r at egy. 7. B u ild t h e c ap acit y o f loc al c o mmu n i t ies a n d gov ern me n t age n c ies, e n ab l in g t h em t o act ively p ar t ic ip a t e i n ma n agin g a n d p r o t ec t in g t h ese ecosys t em s. 1. 2 Pr oject J us t i f i c a t i o n M an gro ves an d t id al salt mar sh es are c ri t ic al eco sy st em s alo n g Gh a n a's c o ast, o f f erin g vit al b en e f it s s u c h as st o rin g c arb o n t o c o mb a t c li mat e c h a n ge, p ro t ect in g b iod iversi t y, an d su p p o rt i n g local livelih o o d s. H o w ever, t h ese ecosys t em s f ace o n goin g t h re at s f ro m h u ma n act ivit ies, c limat e c h an g e imp act s, a n d h ab i t at l o ss, lea d in g t o sign i f ic a n t e n viron m en t al, social an d eco n o mic issu es. Th is p r o je c t a d d r esses t h ese c h all en ges b y gat h erin g c o mp re h en sive d a t a an d d ev elo p i n g p ract ic al st ra t egies t o r est o re an d su st a in a b ly man age t h ese ecosys t e ms. T h is in it iat ive o n al st an d a rd s f o r c arb o n mar k et s, en s u rin g t h at local c o mm u n i t ies b en e f it s o c ially, econ o mically, a n d en vir o n menta lly. 1. 3 Al i gn me n t wit h Na t i onal an d I n t er na t i onal St an da r ds T h is c o n s u lt a n c y w ill ad h ere t o a n d align w it h: a n d st r a teg i e s: In c lu d in g st rategies f o r c limat e re silien c e, c o ast al ma n agem e n t, an d b i o d iversi t y con se rvat i o n. 4 Plan Vivo Sta n d a r d s: Em p h asiz i n g t ra n sp are n t c a rb o n acc o u n t i n g, act ive c o mmu n i t y in volveme n t, b io d iversit y p ro t ect io n, a n d c lea r s o c ial an d eco n o mic b en e f it s. I PCC Gu i d e l i n e s: En s u ri n g sc ien t i f ic ally c re d i b l e meth o d s f o r m ea su ri n g c arb o n st o rage an d em issio n s. Sust a i n a b l e De ve l op m e n t Go a l s (S DG s): Su p p o rt in g glo b al o b je c t ives f o c u sed o n c limat e act ion, mar i n e li f e p r o t ect ion, su st ain a b le c o mmu n it ies, an d p art n ersh ip s f o r su st ain a b le d evel o p me n t. 1. 4 De t ai l ed Pr oje ct Scope Geograph i c Fo cu s: T h e p ro je c t w ill t arget t h e e n t ire c o ast o f t h e c o u n t r y, in c lu d i n g are as t h e So n gor Ram sar Sit e ( V o lt a Est u ary ), Ket a Lagoo n Comp le x, Grea t er Ama n z u le W et la n d s, D e n su D elt a an d t h e M u n i - Pu ma d z e Ramsar Si t e i n Win n eb a, Cen t ral Region. M i n i m u m A r e a f or St u d y: Are as o f at lea st 2 h ect are s w ill t y p ic ally b e p rio ri t iz e d. Sma ller are as w it h st r o n g ecolo gic al c o n n ect ion s o r sign if ic a n t p o t en t ial f o r re st o ra t io n ( min im u m o f 5 h ect are s) may also b e in c lu d e d. Ec ol ogic a l A sp e c ts: D et aile d assessmen t o f ecosys t em ext e n t a n d h ea lt h, b iod iversi t y, c ar b o n se q u es t rat i o n p o t en t ial a n d v u ln e rab ili t y t o e n v iro n me n t al c h an ges. Co m m u n i ty a n d Ec o n o m i c A sp e ct s: Und ers t an d in g an d in t egra t i n g lo c a l livelih o o d s, c u lt u ral p ract ic es, an d p o t e n t i al su st ai n ab l e econ o mic act ivit i es ( lik e s u st ain ab l e f ish in g an d eco - t o u rism). R e st or a ti on Po tent i a l: Id en t i f yi n g d egra d e d are as su it ab l e f o r re st o rat i o n an d c lea rly o u t li n in g t h e m et h o d s a n d b en ef i t s o f r est o ra t io n act ivi t ies. 1. 5 K e y Pr oj ec t Deli v er ab l es 1. Go ve r n m e n t A g e n ci e s: Regu lat o ry o versigh t, t e c h n ic al su p p o rt, an d in v o lveme n t in mo n it o rin g an d eval u at i o n. L oc a l Co m m u n i ti e s a n d CREM A s: Pa rt ic ip at i o n i n d a t a c o ll ect io n, ecosy st em mo n it o rin g, re st o rat i o n act ivit ies, a n d lo n g - t erm su st ain a b ili t y o f t h e p ro j ect. 1. 9 Risk Mana g em en t Pr o act ive id e n t i f ic at i o n an d ma n agem e n t o f risk s re lat in g t o c o mm u n it y in volvem en t, ecosys t em h ea lt h, c lima t e c h a n ge im p act s, a n d d at a re lia b ilit y. S t rategies w ill b e c lea r ly o u t li n ed an d r egu larly re view ed t o e n su re effe c t i ve mit iga t ion. 1. 1 0 Pr oject G o v e r na nc e and M an age me nt T ran sp a re n t p ro je c t gov ern an c e w ill b e est a b lis h ed, c lea rly d ef i n in g ro l es, re sp o n sib ili t ies, an d c o mm u n ic a t io n st r at egies am o n g s t ak eh o ld ers, alig n in g w it h i n t ern at i o n al p ro je c t man agem e n t st a n d ar d s ( PM I). T h is d et ai led an d acc es sib le Pr o je c t Cha r t er est ab lish es a r o b u s t f o u n d at ion f o r t h e B lu e Carb o n Ecosys t em Ass essme n t Con su l t an c y. It en s u re s c lea r u n d e rst an d in g, ac t ive p art ic i p at io n, a n d effe c t i ve execu t i o n, align i n g sc ien t i f ic acc u racy w it h p r act ic al c o mmu n it y en gageme n t an d in t er n a t ion al su s t ain a b ilit y s t an d ard s. 6 1. 8 R oles an d R espon s i bi l i t i es M EST I & M L NR: Pr o j e c t o versigh t, p o lic y gu id an c e, ap p ro vals, a n d re sourc e p ro vis ion. L oc a l Co m m u n i ti e s a n d CREM A s: Pa rt ic ip at i o n i n d a t a c o ll ect io n, ecosy st em mo n it o rin g, re st o rat i o n act ivit ies, a n d lo n g - t erm su st ain a b ili t y o f t h e p ro j ect. 1. 9 Risk Mana g em en t Pr o act ive id e n t i f ic at i o n an d ma n agem e n t o f risk s re lat in g t o c o mm u n it y in volvem en t, ecosys t em h ea lt h, c lima t e c h a n ge im p act s, a n d d at a re lia b ilit y. S t rategies w ill b e c lea r ly o u t li n ed an d r egu larly re view ed t o e n su re effe c t i ve mit iga t ion. 1. 1 0 Pr oject G o v e r na nc e and M an age me nt T ran sp a re n t p ro je c t gov ern an c e w ill b e est a b lis h ed, c lea rly d ef i n in g ro l es, re sp o n sib ili t ies, an d c o mm u n ic a t io n st r at egies am o n g s t ak eh o ld ers, alig n in g w it h i n t ern at i o n al p ro je c t man agem e n t st a n d ar d s ( PM I). T h is d et ai led an d acc es sib le Pr o je c t Cha r t er est ab lish es a r o b u s t f o u n d at ion f o r t h e B lu e Carb o n Ecosys t em Ass essme n t Con su l t an c y. It en s u re s c lea r u n d e rst an d in g, ac t ive p art ic i p at io n, a n d effe c t i ve execu t i o n, align i n g sc ien t i f ic acc u racy w it h p r act ic al c o mmu n it y en gageme n t an d in t er n a t ion al su s t ain a b ilit y s t an d ard s. 7 2.0 Me tho d s an d S t and a r ds 2. 1 I n t r oduct i on t o th e Me t hod s T h is p ro j ect w ill u se a c o mb in a t ion o f mo d er n sc ien t if ic me t h o d s, loc al k n o w led ge, an d c o mmu n i t y in volveme n t t o assess t h e p o t en t ial o f ma n gro ves an d t id al salt mar s h ecosys t em s in Gh a n a t o st o re c arb o n an d su p p o r t local livelih o o d s. T h e met h o d s align w i t h glob ally re c o g n iz e d s t a n d ar d s, sp eci f ic ally Pla n V ivo an d IPCC, t o en su re acc u racy, t ran s p are n c y, a n d c o mm u n it y p ar t ic ip a t ion. 2. 2 De f i ni ng th e Pr oject Sc ope T h e assessme n t w ill c o ver t h e e n t ir e c o ast o f t h e c o u n t ry w it h sp ecif ic i n t er est i n So n go r Ramsar Sit e ( V o lt a Est u ary), Ket a Lagoo n Co mp lex, D en s u D el t a, Grea t er Ama n z u l e Wet lan d s, a n d M u n i - Pumad z e Ramsar Si t e i n Wi n n e b a. D et ail ed map s w ill b e c re at ed t o sh o w exactly w h ic h are as are in c lu d e d an d t h eir en viron menta l st a t u s. Ecosys t em are as c o n sid ere d w ill t ypically b e 2 h ect are s o r large r, b u t smalle r ar ea s w it h h igh r est o ra t ion p o t en t ial ( at l ea st 5 h ect are s o f p o t en t ial re st o re d are a) w ill also b e in c l u d e d. 2. 3 Baseli ne Sc enario Es t ab l i shmen t Ecolo gic al N es t w ill f i rst est ab lis h w h at t h e c o n d i t ion o f t h ese ecosys t em s w o u ld lik ely b e i f n o c o n se rvat io n o r re st o rat io n act i o n s w ere u n d er t ak en. T h is sc en ari o p ro vi d es a c lea r b en c h m ark again st w h ic h t h e p o sit ive im p act s o f f u t u re in t erve n t io n s c an b e mea su re d. T h e b aselin e sc en ari o w ill d et ail c u r re n t ecosys t em h ea lt h, r a t e o f l o ss, c ar b o n s t o rage levels, an d o n g o in g en vir o n men t al p r ess u r es. 2. 4 Ma ppi ng an d E c olog i c al Sur v e y s Ea rt h o b serva t io n t ech n o logy w ill b e u s ed t o c o llect an d a n aly z e d e t aile d c o n d i t io n o f man gro ve a n d t i d al salt mar sh ecosys t em s. T h ese t o o ls w ill h el p ma p exact ecosys t e m b o u n d ari es, h ig h ligh t ar ea s o f d egra d at io n, a n d id e n t i f y locat i o n s i d e al f o r r est o r at io n. Gro u n d t ea ms w ill also vis it t h ese are as t o valid at e sat ellite d at a an d c o n d u c t d e t aile d su rveys o f t h e veg et a t io n, w ild li f e, soil q u alit y, a n d o t h er im p o r t an t eco l o gic al f ea t u r es. 2.5 Ca r bon M easu r em en t an d Acc oun t i ng Fie ld t ea ms w ill t ak e soi l an d veg et a t io n samp l es f ro m t h e ecosys t em s t o mea su re t h e amo u n t o f c ar b o n t h ey s t o re. T h e d a t a c o llect e d w ill t h e n b e u se d t o c alcu la t e h o w mu c h c arb o n is c u r r en t ly s t o r ed an d h o w mu c h a d d i t ional c arb o n c o u ld p o t en t ially be s t o r ed t h r o u gh e f f ect iv e c o n ser v a t io n a n d r es t o r a t io n ac t ion s. 7 2.0 Me tho d s an d S t and a r ds 2. 1 I n t r oduct i on t o th e Me t hod s T h is p ro j ect w ill u se a c o mb in a t ion o f mo d er n sc ien t if ic me t h o d s, loc al k n o w led ge, an d c o mmu n i t y in volveme n t t o assess t h e p o t en t ial o f ma n gro ves an d t id al salt mar s h ecosys t em s in Gh a n a t o st o re c arb o n an d su p p o r t local livelih o o d s. D et ail ed map s w ill b e c re at ed t o sh o w exactly w h ic h are as are in c lu d e d an d t h eir en viron menta l st a t u s. Ecosys t em are as c o n sid ere d w ill t ypically b e 2 h ect are s o r large r, b u t smalle r ar ea s w it h h igh r est o ra t ion p o t en t ial ( at l ea st 5 h ect are s o f p o t en t ial re st o re d are a) w ill also b e in c l u d e d. 2. 3 Baseli ne Sc enario Es t ab l i shmen t Ecolo gic al N es t w ill f i rst est ab lis h w h at t h e c o n d i t ion o f t h ese ecosys t em s w o u ld lik ely b e i f n o c o n se rvat io n o r re st o rat io n act i o n s w ere u n d er t ak en. T h is sc en ari o p ro vi d es a c lea r b en c h m ark again st w h ic h t h e p o sit ive im p act s o f f u t u re in t erve n t io n s c an b e mea su re d. T h e b aselin e sc en ari o w ill d et ail c u r re n t ecosys t em h ea lt h, r a t e o f l o ss, c ar b o n s t o rage levels, an d o n g o in g en vir o n men t al p r ess u r es. 2. 4 Ma ppi ng an d E c olog i c al Sur v e y s Ea rt h o b serva t io n t ech n o logy w ill b e u s ed t o c o llect an d a n aly z e d e t aile d c o n d i t io n o f man gro ve a n d t i d al salt mar sh ecosys t em s. 6.0 R esour ce Manag em en t Plan 6. 1 I n t r oduct i on The R es o u r c e M an ag em en t P lan o u tlin es the h u m an, t echn ic al, an d l o g is tic al r e so u r c es r equ ir ed f o r the suc ces s fu l i m p le m en t a tio n o f the Blu e Carb o n E c o s y s t em Ass ess m en t Co n s u lt an cy. I t p r o v id es a s tructur ed ap p r o ach t o p lan n in g, m o b il iz in g, all o c a tin g, an d m o n it o rin g the r es o u r ces n ee d ed thr o u g h o u t the pr o jec t li f e cy cle. 6. 2 Objecti v es Ensu r e tha t the c o n sul t an c y is ad e q u a t ely r es o u r ced t o d eliv er all o u tpu ts an d d eliv er ab les within t h e 8 - m o n th p r o j ect du r a tio n. Opti m iz e th e u se o f r es o u r ces t o i m p r o v e e f fici enc y a n d m in im iz e w as t e. P r o m o t e a cc o u n t ab il it y an d c lear assig n m en t o f r esp o n sib il ities. 6. 3 Human R es our ce s The p r o j ect will b e i m p l em en t ed b y a m u ltid isci p li n ary t ea m sup p o rt ed b y fi eld t echn icia n s, c o m m u n it y v o lu n t e er s, and k e y s t ak eho ld er s. 7.0 St ak e holder E n g a g em en t a nd Capac it y - B uildi ng Pl an 7. 1 I n t r oduct i on Ef f ec t ive c o n servat ion an d su st ain a b le man ag em en t o f man gr o ve an d t id al salt mar s h ecosys t em s d e p en d o n act ive c o llab o ra t io n a mo n g all st ak e h o ld ers. 7.0 St ak e holder E n g a g em en t a nd Capac it y - B uildi ng Pl an 7. 1 I n t r oduct i on Ef f ec t ive c o n servat ion an d su st ain a b le man ag em en t o f man gr o ve an d t id al salt mar s h ecosys t em s d e p en d o n act ive c o llab o ra t io n a mo n g all st ak e h o ld ers. Co n sensu s - Bui l d i n g M e e ti n g s: En s u re c o m mu n i t y o w n ers h ip a n d ac t iv e in volveme n t. R e st or a ti on A ct i vit i e s: Act ively in volve c o m mu n i t ies in ecolo gic al re st o ra t ion p ro je c t s. S t a k eh ol de r W o r ksho ps: Pr oj e ct Upd a te W or ks h op s: Ke ep s t ak eh o l d ers in f o r med, f acilit a t e f ee d b ack an d in p u t. Str a teg y R e f i n e m e n t W or ksh o p s: Ga t h er i n p u t s t o r ef i n e p ro je c t st ra t egies a n d o u t c o m es. 8.0 Comm un ic a tio ns Mana g em e n t Plan 8. 1 I n t r oduct i on E f f ect i v e c o m m u n ic a tio n is esse n tial t o the succ ess fu l im p le m en t a ti o n o f the Blu e Carb o n E c o s y s t e m Assess m en t C o n sul t an c y.
